NOTE BY THE CONTRIBUTOR:
The text has been wrongly assigned in the VeÇkateÓvara edition 
(and subsequently) to the SkandapurÃïa (i.e. SkP 5.3.); all available 
manuscriptual evidence, however, proves that the text was instead originally
part of the VÃyupurÃïa. Nevertheless in the following text, the original 
colophones referring to the SkandapurÃïa have been retained.
There is a RevÃkhaï¬a of the SkandapurÃïa too, which, however, comprises 
116 adhyÃyas only. That text is almost forgotten; I have also contributed 
an electronic version of that text to GRETIL.
(For further information on this group of texts, please contact the contributor at jneuss@arcor.de.)
